Nice here's a brownie recipe  *Ingredients:* - 1/2 cup (115g) unsalted butter - 1 cup (200g) granulated sugar - 2 large eggs - 1 teaspoon vanilla extract - 1/3 cup (40g) unsweetened cocoa powder - 1/2 cup (65g) all-purpose flour - 1/4 teaspoon salt - 1/4 teaspoon baking powder - Optional: chocolate chips or nuts for added texture!  *Instructions:*  1. Preheat your oven to 350Â°F (175Â°C). Grease a 9x9 inch baking pan. 2. Melt the butter in a medium saucepan. Once melted, remove from heat and stir in sugar, eggs, and vanilla. 3. Beat in cocoa, flour, salt, and baking powder until well blended. If you like, fold in chocolate chips or nuts. 4. Spread the batter evenly in the prepared pan. 5. Bake for 20 to 25 minutes. Do not overcook! They should be soft in the center. 6. Let them cool before cutting into squares.
